å†…å®¹:1. Event Summary in one paragraph. Cash Coupon NFT will be airdropped to holders. Phantabear community will join a community channel ( Community channels are divided according to where the various holders are located. Eg: Singapore, China-Beijing, Taiwan-Taichung, Korea-Seoul etc) and decide a Healthy Lifestyle activity within the community channel. Holders will pay for their own expenses first (cycling, running, rollerblading, rock-climbing, hiking etc). Subsequently they will fill in a claim form online which includes submitting receipt of their expenses + social media link with photograph of themselves attending the event + Cash Coupon NFT to be burnt in order to get reimbursement of the money. 2. Frequency of Cash Coupon NFT airdrop Airdrop will be held once every 2-6 months to allow sufficient increase in the community fund (from royalties). The faster the speed at which the community fund increases, the more frequent we can have this airdrop. The faster the speed at which the community fund increases, the higher the value of Cash Coupon NFT will be airdropped. 3. SNAPSHOT + Cash Coupon NFT Airdrop Snapshot will be taken prior to an airdrop of Cash Coupon NFT (distributed via polygon chain - literally close to no gas required) Holding (In future, staking is required) 1 Phantabear --> you will be airdropped a $10USD NFT Cash Coupon into your Metamask Wallet. Eg: Holding 5 Phantabears = 5 x $10 NFT Cash Coupon Holding (In future, staking is required) 1 PhancyPet --> you will be airdropped a $1USD NFT Cash Coupon into your Metamask Wallet.. Eg: Holding 5 PhancyPet = 5 x $1 NFT Cash Coupon Holding (In future, staking is required) 1 PhancyPet + 1 Phantabear --> you will be airdropped a $15USD NFT Cash Coupon into your Metamask Wallet.. Eg: Holding 6 PhancyPet + 4 Phantabear = 4 x $15 NFT Cash Coupon and 2 x $1 NFT Cash Coupon There is no expiry date for Cash Coupon NFT redemption. 4. How to Utilize the Coupon 4.1 Holders will attend the Group Event and submit claim form to get reimbursement through coupon redemption for the amount they spent. Group Event will have a lucky draw conducted at the end of it. 4.2 They will fill in a claim form online which includes submitting receipts of their expenses + social media link with photograph of themselves attending the event + Cash Coupon NFT to be burnt in order to get reimbursement of the money. Eg: If your combined receipts show that you have spent $22USD (after conversion to USD), and u have submitted 1x$15 and 1x $5 Cash coupon NFT to be burnt, you will be reimbursed with $20USDC into your metamask wallet (polygon chain). But if you have spent $18USD instead, only $18USD will be reimbursed even though you have submitted $20USD worth of Cash Coupon NFT (This is how Coupon works). 4.3 Holders who are unable to attend the planned Group Event to utilize the cash coupon due to geographical issue, can choose to sell their Cash Coupon NFT in the secondary market. 4.4 However, if holders can create a mini-healthy lifestyle gathering event themselves (A minimum of 4 Phantabear participants is required, + unlimited number of non-phantabear participants), they can also utilize the Cash Coupon and submit the claim form for reimbursement. If a holder has a lot of Cash Coupon (eg. $80 worth and they are unable to finish all by themselves, they are allowed to use it to claim for the expenses of the non-phantabear holders. (Exactly like how a typical coupon works). This little action of paying for non-phantabear holders will leave a positive image of the phantabear community. This mini-gathering event however will not be entitled to a lucky draw event. There cannot be multiple claim on a single receipts. 5. Group Event Details Holders who attend the group event will be able to utilize the cash coupon for reimbursement. Group Event will have a lucky draw conducted at the end of it. 5.1. Phantabear and Phancy Pet Holders need to fill in a survey form which will continually update where they are located and where the group event should be held. "Example of survey results: 5200 Phantabear and Phancy Pet Holder: 1000 In china - 100 in beijing - 100 in Chengdu - ..... etc 1000 in Singapore - 1000 in singapore 1000 in Taiwan - 500 in Taipei - 500 in Taichung ........ etc" 5.2 Having identified the best location to hold the Group event at different countries, the holders will join a community channel ( Community channels are divided according to where the various holders are located. Eg: Singapore, China-Beijing, Taiwan-Taichung, Korea-Seoul etc) and decide a Healthy Lifestyle activity within the community channel 5.3 A representative volunteer will submit a simple application form on behalf of the community to claim money for the lucky draw. $10USD/group of 10 Phantabear participants. 5.4. On the event day, participants will meet-up and enjoy the group-event they have planned. At the end of the event they will conduct a lucky draw. (Eg. 1 winner of $10 McDonald's voucher) There must be at least 10 Phantabear holder in a group event in order for the lucky draw claim to be valid. Eg: Inside #Singapore channel The community decided to have a Healthy Lifestyle cycling event. They chose to have a group meet-up of 20pax. 13 holders and 7 non-holders (friends of holders) is expected to attend. One volunteer will submit a simple application form to get $10USD for the group lucky draw. Participants spent $13 each on bicycle rental. Subsequently at the end of the cycling event, a lucky draw is conducted to decide the winner of the $10USD among the 20pax. Some of the participants decided to grab some lunch among themselves. Because they have attended a Group Event, they are allowed to use their Cash Coupon to even claim for a lunch or dinner within the same day provided they show photograph proof that it is used for community bonding. If a holder has a lot of Cash Coupon (eg. $200 worth and they are unable to finish all by themselves, they are allowed to use it to claim for the expenses of the non-phantabear holders. (Exactly like how a typical coupon works). This little action of paying for non-phantabear holders will leave a positive image of the phantabear community. As example, John (a whale with $200 cash coupon NFT) is among the 13 holders to attend the cycling event and has invited 3 friends (non-holders among the 7 non-holders). At the end of the Group event, he decided to have lunch with these 3 friends of his. Another non-holder also decided to join for lunch. The five of them spent $118 on lunch together. John is allowed to use his Cash Coupon NFT to get reimbursement of the cycling expenditure ($13x4=$52) and lunch ($118). There cannot be multiple claim on a single receipts.

Event Details: -Every 3 month, we will create a poll for all holders to vote on which NFT project to invest in. -Every 3 months, we will evaluate our NFT investment portfolio. Rationale: -Some community members may feel that other NFT projects have more potential than Phantabear in the shorter terms: Azuki, BAYC, Cyberbrokers etc. -Through investing by holding established blue chip NFT in community wallet, we become a shareholder indirectly of other projects -This will increase our community DAO for future community events: --- When our investment increases in value, our community DAO increases in value in terms of number of eth; --- When phantabear floor price starts to increase in value, our community DAO will have increase with more royalty from sale transaction. -Let our community money grow and use them when we need to liquidate for community event. When the community collectively make investment decision together, we will be more bonded together and we will get rich together.

Mechanism to Earn Phantaseed: 1. Daily check-in with the #bot inside discord 2. Participating and attending community events: Singing, games, meet-up etc 3. Talking positively inside the community - admin/mod/developer have the power to reward Phantaseed accordingly with justification. We will not penalize by removing a holder's phantaseed. 4. Rather than issuing Whitelist for all to click and raffle (including fudders), all WL spot raffle will require holders to use the Phantaseed token to purchase the raffle ticket in order to participate in the raffle (this will eliminate fudder) (So far the projects WL that we have are top-notch, everyone wants to win WL) 2. Phantaseed can also be used to redeem community titles - that will have more future utility within the discord community. Eg: those with the title will get a chance to _________ (to be decided along the way). 3. Accumulating sufficient Phantaseed over months will enable you to redeem a phantabear NFT or other physical rewards not limited to online cash voucher (purchased using the community wallet). The number of Phantaseeds required have to be extremely extremely high of course. 4. Redeeming a fractal of *Community Phantabear NFT. .... and more to be announced in the future Note: Phantaseed is an INCENTIVE for the community to grow, not a tool/mechnism for others to demand to be paid. *Community Phantabear NFT. Short introduction of this Community Phantabear NFT: -The community will create a community art of Phantabear (with association to growth, lights, charity and positivity) and the best community art will be created as an NFT. -The Community NFT will be broken down into 10 000 pieces termed fractal. -Phantabear holders can redeem a fractal with a fixed number of Phantaseed. -Utility of Community Phantabear NFT Mosaic will be decided in the future. It will be a surprise, I shall not elaborate for now.

æ´»åŠ¨åç§°:Metaverse treasure hunt ARG
æ´»åŠ¨ç›®çš„:PantaBear holders are all over the world. We are everywhere. There is a limit to our meeting on offline. However, there is no limit to our meetings and activities online with Metaverse. And if we have purpose to the encounter and entanglement, the synergy becomes stronger. With fun and rewards, it will bring power beyond all communities in the world. ARG? Alternative Reality Game. It's a game of the way it's linked to reality. ARG players feel immersion as if the event actually happened. It feels like the boundaries between online and offline are collapsing, and members of the community can more and more assimilated with the community. Using the development of Metaverse and Jay Chou's brand power, It creates a reality-like game that everyone can enjoy sitting down to determine the winners who achieved their goals on a first-come, first-served basis. The genre is to perform various quests, solve riddles, and go through the gates one by one to find a treasure. In these games, we will be able to have an indirect experience of the world that PantaBear pursues.
å†…å®¹:- Duration of the event: 1. 48 to 72 hours for short planning with competition mode 2. If everyone plans to follow the story together, it can be done for about a month. - Run-down : 1. Every treasure hunt has a story. Ex) Jay Chou, who had a mysterious accident, lost his most precious thing one day. But Jay Chou has no memory. We got his cell phone records, CCTV records, diary schedules, etc. Now we have to go after his past and investigate what happened and what he lost. 2. Data that's decorated as if it were real evidence is accessible to everyone who is qualified. People can reason and solve riddles. 3. Through such activities, you can get the addresses of places Jay Chou visited in the story (real world addresses) and explore the surroundings with road views through Google Maps. 4. And in the case of a specific place (someone's house, etc.), a place modeled after it is implemented in a metaverse. We can continue the search the evidences in the metaverse through first-person view which is seen through field agent's mounted spy-cam (It's just story setting) 5. The last thing I found was the only PhantaBear in Jay Chou's heart. The End of the long journey - Participation condition : Eligible for every holder of PhantaBear or PhancyPet - Method of participation : Internet - Principles for the winner: 1. In competitive mode, the game ends when the first person passes all gates, and from that point on, the people who enter a particular gate are ranked in chronological order and awarded prizes. 2. In cooperative mode, the person who deduces and solves the riddles or evidence revealed through the progress of the progress team takes the score, and at the end of the game, the person who scores the most is ranked in order.
é¢„ç®—:The expected budget is as follows. - Time and professional employment required for story planning - Labor costs for the progress team - The cost of planning and designing evidence and riddles - Cost of awards - Site and server maintenance costs
å¥–å“:- Awards : * Definite WL or airdrop of future collaboration projects * Physical compensation related to PhantaCi products or Jay Chou * Money (everyone loves money) - Number of Winners: It depends on the number of participants in the game. If the participate size is small, there may be three people, and if the size is large, there may be more than 5 or 10 people
